Finally, Done

2022-03-March-17-Thursday I'ts been a long time since I last wrote my diary, lots of things happened I decided that I'm not going to write until I'm done with my project, and today I was finally done, I think I tested everything, and everything have worked so far. I finally have what I wanted to have 2 years ago, A website where I write and update my projects, my diary, and what I've been up to in general. It's done now, but I'm not going to stop working on it, But I'm going to leave it for a few months, and focus on learning something new. What have I been up to I'm still struggling a bit with spending my time with on my own, but It's getting easier and easier over time, but now I think I have a Different problem. Too much work ? So now that I can't really waste my time talking with other people, Now I spend almost all of my time just working on my project. And I noticed that it's just work that I do, and now I'm having a hard time doing anything else, as soon as I start playing a game or watch something I start thinking, "I should be working right now, I'm wasting time, I need to build skills". It seems like I'm just doing too much of one thing, and Probably making a schedule would be better for me in the future. OverThinker I got a bit confused with how I'm going about my relationship with people, I'm starting to lean more and more towards just totally forgetting about the groups that I use to spend my time with. And maybe go find another, or not find any group at all, and spend the whole of my time or at least most of it by my self. Sometimes it seems like my friends don't really like me, and I'm not sure if that's just me overthinking stuff or not, sometimes it seems to me like my friends usually tend to avoid me more than not. It could be just me in the end, I do have a history of over thinking things after All Fuck windows So Uni started, and I only have to go there 2 days a week only, and that's good and all, but 2 of my courses want me to use C# and Microsoft Visual Studio (not Visual Studio Code). And this means I have to switch from Linux to windows, and this might not seem like a problem, but it turned out to be a bit annoying. It toke me 2 days, because I had to change my Hard Drive's File system, Which means I had to back up all my data, thankfully I had an external Hard Drive, and that toke almost all day to copy. Then I had to install windows, which I hated, I don't have my shortcuts , I don't have my virtual desktops, I can't customize my desktop look. And to be honest, I don't really know what people like about windows anymore, cuz It does things really slowly compared to linux. Other than some games and some software, I don't know why people like windows too much, All We need is to make linux More user friendly (it already is), and I think the move would be much easier. Things are looking good Now that I'm done with the project, I made a video about it today, and I just need to edit it and uploaded. And I'm going to be using it to update my portfolio on github, it's going to make things way easier to do now than what it used to be. I'm planing to learn a few things in the next few months, and see if I'm going to stick to one of them or just I'm going to keep working with multiple things at once. I have some high hopes for the next few months, things will get better.

Pain

2022-02-February-26-Saturday Been uneventful today, I tried to work, and managed to do something, still not as much as I would like to do, but as keep saying some progress is better than no progress. Starting to leave So I think I'll keep on slowly getting out of the communities that I'm currently in, I'm probably gonna stay in one or two but not any more than that. I'm also planing to only keep communicating with important friends, and maybe not do too much of that too, hopefully this would free up more time. Lurking I'm still thinking that some of my friends are avoiding me now, I'm not exactly sure about it, but I'll try to delay my judgment on that, I'm still also not sure why, and to me, they don't seem to want me around. Now, I totally can write this as me being the hero, but I probably did something without noticing it, and I really want to keep things as is, so I'm gonna try my best to wire what actually happened Weird one Weird thing is yesterday I tried to join one of my friends, and they refused, but because of how buggy the game was, I decided to ask if I had a bad timing or if they didn't receive my request. They said I had bad timing, but I could still text them, and fair enough, decided not to keep bothering them, but then they sort of started asking me about feeling, which is normal actually. They usually ask me questions about my mental, and I do answer those as accurate as I can, and sometimes that's just how we talk. Emotional ? And it felt like I'm ... being interrogated or something, again this could be my judgment being cloudy, but that's how it seemed to me at the time. Also found it a bit weird, when it's not a good timing for me to be there (I was trying to join them in vrchat), but still kept talking to me. All this is kinda enforcing that ... maybe my friends are trying to avoid me, and I'm not about to go around and say it's not my fault, it actually could be, but I really don't know. Shaky judgment At the time I'm writing this, I'm not sure if I should try again to be honest, cuz then I might end up making the thing worse, it's not like I hate them, but I'm emotional currently, and I could do something stupid. And been thinking maybe this is the best choice I have, so I'll keep on doing it, and see where this goes, I still can keep my most important communications going, still I'll be a bit sad if I lose more friends. Resisting I've been kinda lurking everywhere, not sure if I should cancel the plan and just act like nothing happened, and go talk to my friends, but I kept on fighting this desire all day. As much as I enjoy the company, it could be one of the reasons things are not going as well as I wish they are, maybe I could be using it as an excuse for not doing things. Or it could be just bad for me all together, So I'll keep on fighting though this pain, and hope that it does not totally break me, I can say that it's not a fun process at all. Mental I'm still kinda depressed, and I feel a bit exhausted from the past few days, I'm starting to get some headaches too, not sure what's that about, and I'm having a lot of mixed thoughts. Are the friends I made so far really are my friends ? Do I keep on just leaving everyone on the hopes that I don't get attached to anyone again ? Is it even the right thing to do ? Or is this going to end up with me going mad ? Who are my important friends? How do I know them ? Will I ever find a group I belong to? Am I already there and don't realize it yet? Am I just trapped in this process of finding and leaving people? Convincing my self, every time, that this is where I stay? Is my work just for nothing, and am I just doomed to fail? Those questions are raising a massive amount of anxiety, and a little bit of anger and pain, Hope that going through this would help me be someone better. This and also feeling undesirable, it not a really fun place to be at, and ... I don't think I can even get to complain, I thought I won't be dealing with this feeling again, but here I am. Never again, I'll be getting close to people or allowing them to get close to me, maybe it is just how life is, and so be it, I'll stick to my games, work, and tools, see how long this can last before I can't continue anymore. I'll keep on going, but still, it's very painful.

A hit

2022-02-February-25-Friday Did not do much today, I made pizza dough preparing for the next week or maybe few days, and this toke me quite a lot of time, I'm not good at it XD, but usually the end result is good. I tried to work, but also got distracted a lot, tried to play games at first, didn't work well, so I tried to get to work, got few things fixed, and worked on the design too. Not as much work as I would like to do, but some work, some progress is better than no progress, I'll be trying to do more and hope that it goes well. Doubts Today I've been heavy on the emotional side of things, been thinking about the few things that happened this week : I made one of my friends angry for discussing something, and noticed that every discussion we had led to them getting more and more frustrated towards me. I made another friend upset with me, because it seemed for them like I was talking all by my self, while for me it seemed like I was just trying to explain in detail, both of those could be true at the same time, but at least they told me, and I know that maybe I should limit the amount of time I take to talk about something. I'm also being a bit annoyed at how I'm being treated in some places, and decided to leave those places, it got a bit ridiculous, so I decided it's probably time to leave, and to be honest I'm not planing to come back. I'm also not sure if my friends really want me to be around, I know some of them do, but it's starting to look like people starting to get upset with me, which is fair enough, cuz there is a higher chance that I'm the crazy one there. Those things are starting to make me doubt if I can solve the problems assuming they are my fault, while at the same time being a bit confused to where I made a mistake in some of them. And it's making me think if I want to keep on maintaining as many things as I have right now, for me, it seems a lot, and most of those problems are social ones, and I don't want to just run away from the problem. I'm starting to think that it's time to actually lower the social connections I have, and focus more on what to work on, like projects, and only the important relationships that I have. Limiting my time even more when it comes to spending it with people, and maybe stop trying to make new friends, so can focus enough on the work I do, while keeping my connections maintained. This might end up hurting some of the people that I know now, but going to ... forget about and move on, but I think I have to choose this, because I have to look after my self too. I'm sorry, but if I want to fix my life, I need to do this Emotional These things are giving me a mix of emotions, I think it's getting me again, and I may not be thinking straight, so may not be the best decision. Depressed and upset So, some of my friends are upset with me, and I can't exactly find out why, I'm gaining even more weight, my sleep schedule is not how I want it to be. I'm not being as productive as I want, I'm not building good habits, My bad habits are taking over, things are not shaping up very well. Those things are just messing with me, because I'm trying to find out about my fuckups, while at the same time keeping with my projects, and it's kinda draining. It could be that I'm doing too much at once, and lowering the load of one part, well ease doing the other parts, and that could be what I need to do. It's not that I want to leave because I'm depressed and I need a break and the world is evil, but it's because I'm starting to think I'm trying to pick up a heavier load than I can actually carry. So I'm gonna hope that I did the right thing and go with it, it's really hard to know those things for sure, it's almost impossible so, I'll try to focus on the progress, and hope for the best. Hope that it goes well.

Podcast is back.

2022-02-February-17-Thursday Today, I was planning to work on the project, get done with the permission system, but I was really lazy, and decided that I'm not going to do that, just spent sometime playing games. Rusty boys Was able to get a hold of my podcast buddy, and I decided that we're going to do a podcast today, and I think it went well. We go with the flow We just started talking like normal, kinda winging it, and I think it went fine, At the begging it was pretty slow, and it seemed like it's not heading anywhere. Topic : Sins and humility But, it was actually fine, and talked about humility in religions, and that the job of humility is to remind us about our imperfection, that we are in fact sinful. The good person delusion And we seem to forget about our mistakes so easily, because we don't want to see ourselves as bad people, and to protect ourselves we make excuses. But, this end up making us worse people in the end, ignoring our mistakes, thinking that we are better than everyone else, because we're blinded from our's. The humility solution Humility helps solving that problem, because we admit to ourselves of our own sins/mistakes, while also admitting it to god, and we ask for forgiveness. When we admit those sins to our selves, we also see our selves as we actually are, imperfect, and sinful, focusing our attention on our actions and hopefully fixing our behavior. The aftermath I enjoyed the podcast a lot to be honest, we are planing to do another one soon too, if we get to, I really hope we do. A problem When I was done with the recording I decided to edit the video, and maybe publish it at the same day, but unfortunately didn't finish editing the video yet. And I found a problem as I was watching it my self, and for some reason my microphone was making a weird humming sound, through the whole recording. And that's going to make editing the video a nightmare at some point, but it is what it is, and I'll try to finish it tomorrow, and also add it to the journal. Something new I also decided to meet one of my friends in vrchat tonight, and I ended meaning new person, they seem fine, and maybe a new friend, they seem â€œchillâ€, maybe I'll be making a new friend soon. Trying to do better I want to do more things to be honest, I should try to fix my sleep, and I should try to be more productive, if possible, and finish the project as soon as I can. I'll try to do that in the next few days. Things gonna be getting better, I hope.

More Frustration

Trying to learn something new Today I was trying to work on a software called "pipewire", and it's supposed to be a sound server system, that can handle everything that is making sounds in the operating system. It does that, I think it does it pretty well to be honest, the problem was with the customization part of it. The good part Pipewire is an open source software, which is good, it opens makes it so that other people who are experienced in coding, able to change and customize the software. And that was what I was trying to do, the problem is pipewire is still in â€œearlyâ€ stages of development, and even tho it does its job well, It's still missing a few things here and there, but I can for the most part work without it. The annoying part After a few hours of reading, or at least trying to read and understand the documentation of that software, I was even more confused about how to customize it. Fuck pipewire The documentation is not good its allover the place, and it does not have good examples, it does not have a table of all the commands and what they do. It does not really explain everything which is bad, and that is making me think of my project and writing good documentations for it. Lesson learned It shows that, even if you made a really good software made and made it free, if you don't document it very well, it's almost useless. I'll try to look for what other people might have done to do what I'm trying to do with my setup. The potential If I somehow manage to do it right, I might end up with perfect configurations, that anyone can use for video/audio production purposes, or just a better control over the sound in a Linux system, which might at least help people migrating. Mental health I've been kinda weird the past few weeks, and I'm swinging between feeling lonely and angry, I still miss my friends and I feel bad for their situations. I'm being more of a â€œfeelingâ€ kind of person than I would like to be, it seems to affect my productivity, to be honest, I'm not sure how I'm going to handle it. But I'm trying to keep on working I'm going to try to keep on moving, getting things done, learning new things. And I do get to good points every now and then, I guess that's just how it is, probably that's just life, and I'm not realizing it. Ignored, or just paranoid. Been trying to communicate with a friend recently, and ... it seems like they are ignoring me, I know that they might be going through some tough time. Situations like those get me a bit paranoid I guess, However, and to be fair to my friends, I also struggle with keeping up with people, and replying to them. I'm not perfect in my self, and It's not like I'm the first priority in anyone's life, things are more complicated of course. I guess writing this is not to show that I â€œknow thingsâ€, it's more like me checking my sanity. Things to work on So I'm planning to keep working on the permission system, it's getting close, I need to make it so that the permissions can be edited, and make a new user group. Make sure that promoting groups won't brake the permissions priorities, and I need to make sure that permissions can't be given on one level, then moved to a higher level than the â€œpromoterâ€ can assign that permission for.

The doomer mentality I've seen a video about what we call now the "doomer", which is a term referring to a person that has lost hope in his/her life, mostly a male, and in a situation where they see themselves are losers or failures. And that the problem in what most of what people do to try to help the "doomer", is that they sort of look at his/her problems from their wont prospective, other than looking at it from the "doomer"'s prospective. And in a way or another, that could mean that they don't really want to help the "doomer", they just want to appear to want to help. And the problem of the "doomer" is, people would suggest solutions for him, but what they don't see, that the "doomer" can't see the value of what they might get from that "solution", because the "doomer" situation is way more complicated than just one solution. They just don't see the complicity of it, the "doomer" can see the possible value of those "solutions", but those "solutions" well require a different "situation" if you well or "environment" for them to actually show any kind of improvement to their life. there probably is a way to "help" the "doomer", but it's not not going to be easy I kinda wanna talk about this topic sometime soon so I'll just add it to a to-do list

Terror of the monster within

2021-10-October-03-Sunday It's been interesting and a bit scary few days, few things happened that i sort of couldn't make up my mind on how I'm going to write about it, so I put them on wait, but I think now is good enough. Facing the monster within Few days ago I had a situation, where my mother got into my room, and she started telling both me and my brother, to stop doing what we were doing and do our praying duties. I told here â€œmom, now it's not the time, please close the door.â€ She refused, â€œno, get up now, don't talk to me like that, it's disrespectful.â€ I repeated, slightly irritated, â€œmom, it's not the time, please close the door.â€ She refused again, â€œdon't say that, it's disrespectful.â€ I repeated, really irritated, â€œmom, really, it's not the time for this, leave the room, and close the door.â€ She refused, again, â€œdon't talk to me like ...â€ At that point, I snapped and said, loudly and aggressively, â€œCLOSE THE DOOR!!â€ She got scared and left and closed the door. What actually happened So this is going back a long time ago, but I'm just going to give a good enough background, to understand what actually happened. My religion is Islam, and in Islam we are required to do a lot of things, but the most important duty is to do 5 prayers a day. And my mom always keep demanding that I do them, and I would really do them, if she leave me be. How I think things are From her view she still sees me as a child, and I'm thinking that she's afraid of me growing up, and becoming independent, some people may think that's ridicules, but that's a real condition. A mother would be way overprotective, that she wonâ€™t let her child go outside without her, if they leave she HAS TO KNOW where they are going and for how long, and would mostly be against any acts of exploration, taking risks, or do anything that have a chance of harming the child, and the idea of her child or children leave the house and live alone would be terrifying for her, so that she don't face that terror she makes the child dependent on her, even if it end up making the child miserable. My mom was sort of overprotective, not to the max but also very noticeable, she wouldn't let me try to do things that are sort of out of the â€œnormâ€ with my classmates, or just trying a hobby that could hurt me physically, she won't let me play outside with my friends, she would tell me to play with my friend in the house. At some point I used to go to a karate dojo, I had a practice that end up inflicting pain on me, and I was tarting to think, I don't want to go there anymore, and I don't remember if that even happened, but I would bet that my mom supported that I stop going there so that I don't get harmed. I remember the master, called my dad and literary told him, if money is an issue, we'll keep training him for free. Unfortunately I decided to top going. That decision has its own story, so when I talk about it, I'll link it here. And she always tries to sort of make decisions for me, try to take control of what I do and how I do it, and when I do it. Which makes the child dependent even more on the mother to take control, making the child unable to take care of him/her self later on, or take responsibility of anything he/she do. And she always says, â€œoh in the future you are going to grow up and probably get married and leave me here alone.â€, another sign that she was overprotective, and probably would rather I don't grow up. situation getting worse At some point, she was always going into my room, and changing how things are arranged , or maybe do the bed and clean the room, and you would think I would be grateful for that, but there was nothing that could make me even more angry, than going back to my room, after a day of â€œcollage/workâ€ only to find it different from how I left it, and some things probably are lost. I wanted to do clean my room my self, her doing that for me, is her not letting me take responsibility, and making me even more useless and hopeless and depressed. So I used to fight her almost every day, telling here don't get into my room, and at some point i told her â€œI'm welling to burn the whole house with everyone in it, if you get into my room again.â€ I still think I probably would have done it, so decided to lock the room door, she cried, which is a tactic that she keeps using to this day, to make me change my mind, that no longer work on me. She doesn't clean my room any more I do that my self, but it took me a long time to fight here This been long, but that's what has been happening, I was already a bit irritated, my parents never knock on my door before they enter the room still, she's probably thinking that I'm becoming independent on her now, cuz I know how to clean my room cook for my self, fix some issues in the house , I'm learning to find a job, and I'm not spending as much time with her anymore. So she has been demanding that I do my prayers, and I get angry every time ,and tell her ,that she needs to leave me be, cuz what she's doing is making me hate doing my duties, and I'll do them my self eventually, she just has to leave me in peace. She always says that she's afraid that she will be judged for not telling me, and I told her that at my age, and the stage we are, she is no longer responsible for what I do. And again told her that she should leave me alone, and I would be happy to help her with things that she want from me, but not anything that is only my responsibility. how things went down That same day she tried to tell again, and I told her, you're making me even more mad, please leave me be. And then it happened She comes to my room, I'm already irritated, she demands that I stop what I'm doing, and do as she tells me, I tell her, it's not the time, and she should leave and close the door. She ignores me few times, playing on the â€œdisrespectâ€ game, finally snap and shout, "CLOSE THE DOOR" that shout was really aggressive. Facing madness I started thinking , almost 30 min after what happened, about what actually happened. And for a bit, I was sort of thinking, that was not me, then in my mind I said, no that definitely was me, getting just a little bit closer to madness, that is for sure the part of me that really don't want to take over, who knows what I might have done At that moment, if I was poked even more, or if I just didn't resist the desire of destroying everything thing that annoys me even a little. That is the part that most people are ignorant of, thinking that they are good people, that won't do any harm, that they won't dislike their children, that they won't harm their significant other. They say "oh no, I'm not a monster", but as a smart man once said "you are a monster, but you're just an unbelievably naive monster, which is the most harmful type" I don't want to end up the person who harms my family. After the storm So after few hours I decided I have to go talk to my mother, but this time I decide I'll have to do all the talk so that, we don't end up having this happening again. I told her, that I never want or mean to shout at her, or scare her, but also she needs to be careful with what she says to me, we already had a discussion about that topic, and I'm getting sick of it, and you better leave me be; because of you don't leave me be, I might just go mad, and who knows what might happen then, I might harm my self, I might harm you, who knows I might even end up killing you, we heard about stories like that all the time with other people around us. you have to be careful when you poke me, I may have patience, but it's never enough to take everything, I know that I should respect you and be nice with you, and I'm trying to be, but you have to help me do that too, please don't just keep on poking me, thinking that nothing should ever happen, and that i should just take that without suddenly snapping , cuz that not helpful and doesn't work I'll be trying to be more patient, but also you need to respect my privacy, and leave me to deal with my own "business/issues", if I want to talk about it, I'll come to you my self, you don't force your well on me, cuz that well make me resentful, and push me to madness, and god only knows what happens when we get there, but it won't be good for any of us. I don't want to hate you, I don't hate you, but don't make me. You have to let us take responsibility, or we will get more and more irritated, and hate each other more and more Fear of falling into madness What made me think that I'm sure that things won't end up good if this happens again. I sort of remember looking at my mother, but it's like I didn't recognize her at that stage, It's as if she was "some random object that is annoying me more than I can endure", and that I can just get up and destroy that object, I just have to get up and start attacking, with the intent to kill and destroy. I was blinded by madness, who know what I would do after this, and I started to get scared of my self, thinking that at any point someone could provoke me the wrong way, and if I don't communicate that the need to stop, or they refuse to stop, I might end up harming them badly. Seeking guidance Then I went back to my room, and tried to sleep, but I couldn't, I wanted to write about it, so I wrote about it to a friend, and we talk about it, and exchanged some thoughts. It was risky; cuz I never know if they just view me as a very horrible person with that story, and decide to never talk to me again. I'm thinking of sharing this with another friend, I'm sort of not totally sure what to think about it. There are few more things I want to talk about tomorrow, a way more bright than today's story. Looking forward to talk about it. But that's going to be it for today Hope that my mom stop trying to control my life, and make decisions for me, allow me to grow up and be less miserable. Doing the big think

2021-02-February-02-Tuesday So today I actually didn't do any progress to my website, I don't know why tbh I got distracted with games actually . But I also was thinking about a Project/2D physics engine/Introduction project, I want to make it so that it's as optimized as possible, so that's going to take a lot of time again I'm planing to work on it for the next 5 years. I want things like cloth simulation, fluid dynamics â€œwater simulationâ€, destructive objects, friction, attaching and detaching â€œobjectsâ€ to each other, gravity. almost everything I can think of. So I ran into the problem of choosing the â€œbestâ€ programming language for the task, and so far it seems like C is the best for this. The reason that I say the â€œbestâ€ programming language and why I would have to learn a new one has to do with the purpose of the programming language itself and also how fast it actually works. Some programming languages are made for applications, some are made for systems, some are made for websites. And some of them are â€œeasierâ€ to get work done with than others. that depends on the level of the language. High level are used in applications and such, low levels are used for systems. but generally it means the languages itself deals with the hardware in a â€œspecific way" lower level languages communicate with hardware better. And that means I would have much better understanding of what kind of resources I'm using. But that means I have to learn a different way of programming. So i what I'm used to is Objects Oriented Programming(OOP), which ties data with objects, this may result in different objects having the same kind of data but a different variable, that are going to be made in different times during the execution. Data Oriented Programming Deals with data that is already known what it's going to be and separates it from â€œfunctions" or operations that are going to be applied on this data, and you won't need to make different â€œObjectsâ€ that have similar â€œpropertiesâ€ that are going to be handled in different stages. The data can be used sort of â€œgloballyâ€ so you wouldn't need to make variables inside the objects. Resulting in dealing with less unnecessary work. Maybe It's going to also be easier to clean the memory from the â€œno longer neededâ€ data in the memory. And after so far after the small research I've done, it seems like C is going to be the best language I can use for the task for now. And in the next few weeks I'm going to try to have that happening, and I'll try to make a small play area. And have a â€œboxâ€ fall, and I'll see where it goes from there. So yeah, I got distracted with those 2 things. Tomorrow my plan is to make the log-in/sign-up page for the user and maybe make the "edit | delete | followâ€ option for the posts, and making dragging and dropping pictures a thing Hopefully I'll get that done tomorrow I'll try to work more actually . But other than that, nothing happened.
